country_event = { #Just southern thrac strip because of ottomans keeping korcha and then giving salonika to greece, also strip
	id = 191334
	title = "Southern Thrace"
	desc = ""
	picture = "crimean_war_russian_victory"
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
        name = "It is clearly Greek land."
		825 = { secede_province = THIS }
		825 = { secede_province = GRE }
		random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    TUR = { owns = 3613 }
                }
            }
            owner = {
				3613 = { secede_province = THIS }
				3613 = { secede_province = GRE }
			}
        }
		829 = { secede_province = THIS }
		829 = { secede_province = GRE }
		#armenia
    }

	option = {
        name = "Leave it in Ottoman hands."
		#armenia
    }

}
country_event = { #Just southern macedonia strip because of ottomans keeping korcha
	id = 191333
	title = "Southern Macedonia"
	desc = ""
	picture = "crimean_war_russian_victory"
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
        name = "It is clearly Greek land."
		820 = { secede_province = THIS }
		820 = { secede_province = GRE }
		821 = { secede_province = THIS }
		821 = { secede_province = GRE }
		831 = { secede_province = THIS }
		831 = { secede_province = GRE }
		805 = { secede_province = THIS }
		805 = { secede_province = GRE }
		822 = { secede_province = THIS }
		822 = { secede_province = GRE }
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = bulgarian_rumelia }
					NOT = { has_global_flag = russian_rumelia }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				country_event = 191334
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_global_flag = albanian_pristina
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = bulgarian_rumelia
						has_global_flag = russian_rumelia
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				country_event = 191332
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = albanian_pristina }
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = bulgarian_rumelia
						has_global_flag = russian_rumelia
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				#armenia
			}
		}
    }

	option = {
        name = "Leave it in Ottoman hands."
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_global_flag = albanian_pristina
				}
			}
			owner = {
				country_event = 191332
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = albanian_pristina }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				#armenia
			}
		}
    }

}

    }

		country_event = 19513

		diplomatic_influence = { who = MOL value = 200 }
		relation = { who = MOL value = 200 }
		MOL = { government = colonial_company }
		create_vassal = WAL
		diplomatic_influence = { who = WAL value = 200 }
		relation = { who = WAL value = 200 }
		WAL = { government = colonial_company }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
    }

    option = {
        name = "Unite them but keep them Ottoman."
		country_event = 19514
		WAL = { annex_to = URP }
		MOL = { annex_to = URP }
		TUR = { create_vassal = URP }
		URP = { government = prussian_constitutionalism }
		diplomatic_influence = { who = URP value = 200 }
		relation = { who = URP value = 200 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
    }

    option = {
        name = "Romania will be united."
		country_event = 1951
		WAL = { annex_to = ROM }
		MOL = { annex_to = ROM }
		diplomatic_influence = { who = ROM value = 200 }
		relation = { who = ROM value = 200 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
    }

country_event = {
	id = 847295
	title = "The Battle of Pkozd"
	desc = "PAKOZDBATTLE"
	picture = "pakozd"
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "ljen Magyarorszg!"
		set_country_flag = hungarian_revolution_began
		small_arms = 100
		regular_clothes = 100
		define_general = { name = "Jzef Bem" personality = defence_3.1 background = attack_1.1 }
		define_general = { name = "Jnos Mga" personality = no_personality background = attack_3.1 }
		define_general = { name = "Mr Perczel" personality = defence_1.1 background = attack_1.1 }
		define_general = { name = "Artr Grgei" personality = defence_2.1 background = attack_minus_1.1 }
		define_general = { name = "Gyrgy Klapka" personality = defence_1.1 background = no_background }
		define_general = { name = "Jnos Damjanich" personality = defence_2.1 background = attack_2.1 }
		define_general = { name = "Lajos Aulich" personality = defence_minus_1.1 background = attack_2.1 }
		define_general = { name = "Kroly Vcsey" personality = no_personality background = attack_2.1 }
		define_general = { name = "Andrs Gspr" personality = defence_1.1 background = attack_2.1 }
		define_general = { name = "Henryk Dembinski" personality = defence_1.1 background = attack_2.1 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = begin_revolution
			duration = 365
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = { has_pop_culture = hungarian }
			militancy = -8
		}
		any_owned = {
			limit = { is_core = ROM }
			any_pop = {
				limit = { has_pop_culture = romanian }
				militancy = 6
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = nationalist_agitation
				duration = 1095
			}
		}
		any_owned = {
			limit = { is_core = SER }
			any_pop = {
				limit = { has_pop_culture = serb }
				militancy = 6
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = nationalist_agitation
				duration = 1095
			}
		}
		AUS = {
			war = {
				target = HUN
				attacker_goal = {
					casus_belli = annex_core_country
				}
				call_ally = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = slovaks_are_mad
		set_country_flag = serbs_are_mad
	}
}

#After US has won the Spanish-American War, they get event 37741 in SPAFlavor.txt
#Option 2 of 3 there lets them decide to occupy Cuba for a couple years (historical)
#This event is Cuba asking for independence in 1902
country_event = {
	id = 16061934
	title = "The Cuban Constitution"
	desc = "CUBACONST"
	picture = "estrada_palma"

    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
		tag = USA
		has_country_flag = cuban_occupation
		owns = 2209
		year = 1902
		CUB = { exists = no }
	}

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = {
        name = "Force them to integrate the Platt Amendment. RGain 1 infamy!"
		badboy = 1
		release_vassal = CUB
		3660 = { secede_province = THIS }
		44 = { secede_province = THIS }
        relation = {
            who = CUB
            value = 200
        }
        diplomatic_influence = {
            who = CUB
            value = 200
        }
		CUB = {
			government = democracy
			political_reform = universal_voting
			political_reform = secret_ballots
		}
	}
	option = {
        name = "Cuba is ready for independence."
		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				is_core = CUB
			}
			secede_province = CUB
		}
		3660 = { secede_province = THIS }
		44 = { secede_province = THIS }
        relation = {
            who = CUB
            value = 200
        }
        diplomatic_influence = {
            who = CUB
            value = 200
        }
		CUB = {
			government = democracy
			political_reform = universal_voting
			political_reform = secret_ballots
		}
	}
}
